```
            var collapsedGroups = JSON.parse(
                localStorage.getItem('collapsedGroups'),
            )

            if (collapsedGroups === null || collapsedGroups === 'null') {
                localStorage.setItem(
                    'collapsedGroups',
                    JSON.stringify([]),
                )
            }

            collapsedGroups = JSON.parse(
                localStorage.getItem('collapsedGroups'),
            )

            document
                .querySelectorAll('.fi-sidebar-group')
                .forEach((group) => {
                    if (
                        !collapsedGroups.includes(group.dataset.groupLabel)
                    ) {
                        return
                    }

                    // Alpine.js loads too slow, so attempt to hide a
                    // collapsed sidebar group earlier.
                    group.querySelector(
                        '.fi-sidebar-group-items',
                    ).style.display = 'none'
                    group
                        .querySelector('.fi-sidebar-group-collapse-button')
                        .classList.add('-rotate-180')
                })
        

        
    

    



            
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        let activeSidebarItem = document.querySelector(
                            '.fi-main-sidebar .fi-sidebar-item.fi-active',
                        )

                        if (
                            !activeSidebarItem ||
                            activeSidebarItem.offsetParent === null
                        ) {
                            activeSidebarItem = document.querySelector(
                                '.fi-main-sidebar .fi-sidebar-group.fi-active',
                            )
                        }

                        if (
                            !activeSidebarItem ||
                            activeSidebarItem.offsetParent === null
                        ) {
                            return
                        }

                        const sidebarWrapper = document.querySelector(
                            '.fi-main-sidebar .fi-sidebar-nav',
                        )

                        if (!sidebarWrapper) {
                            return
                        }

                        sidebarWrapper.scrollTo(
                            0,
                            activeSidebarItem.offsetTop -
                                window.innerHeight / 2,
                        )
                    }, 10)
                })
```

# Test source

```ts
  244 | // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  245 | test('Stage 4 — Intake Assessment', async ({ page }) => {
  246 |   await login(page);
  247 |   await goto(page, `${BASE}/admin/intake-queues`);
  248 |   await lwWait(page, 1000);
  249 |   await snap(page, '04-intake-queue');
  250 | 
  251 |   const row = page.locator('table tbody tr').filter({ hasText: new RegExp(LAST, 'i') }).first();
  252 |   if (await row.isVisible({ timeout: 6000 }).catch(() => false)) {
  253 |     const btn = row.locator('button, a').filter({ hasText: /intake|assess|start/i }).first();
  254 |     if (await btn.isVisible({ timeout: 2000 }).catch(() => false)) {
  255 |       await btn.click();
  256 |     } else {
  257 |       await row.locator('a').first().click();
  258 |     }
  259 |     await lwWait(page, 1000);
  260 |   } else {
  261 |     console.log('ℹ️  Not in intake queue — trying intake-assessments/create');
  262 |     await goto(page, `${BASE}/admin/intake-assessments/create`);
  263 |     await lwWait(page, 1000);
  264 |   }
  265 | 
  266 |   await snap(page, '04-intake-form');
  267 | 
  268 |   const textAreas: [string, string][] = [
  269 |     ['Reason for Visit', 'Client referred for physiotherapy following road traffic accident.'],
  270 |     ['Current Concerns', 'Shoulder pain and reduced range of motion for 3 months.'],
  271 |     ['Previous Interventions', 'None reported.'],
  272 |     ['Assessment Summary', 'Physiotherapy assessment and 6-week programme required.'],
  273 |     ['Recommendations', 'Refer to Physiotherapy Department for initial assessment.'],
  274 |   ];
  275 | 
  276 |   for (const [label, val] of textAreas) {
  277 |     try {
  278 |       const f = page.getByLabel(label).first();
  279 |       if (await f.isVisible({ timeout: 2000 })) {
  280 |         await f.fill(val);
  281 |         await page.waitForTimeout(150);
  282 |       }
  283 |     } catch { /* optional field */ }
  284 |   }
  285 | 
  286 |   await snap(page, '04-intake-filled');
  287 | 
  288 |   await page.getByRole('button', { name: /Save|Create|Submit/i }).first().click();
  289 |   await lwWait(page, 2500);
  290 |   await snap(page, '04-intake-saved');
  291 | 
  292 |   const body = await page.locator('body').textContent();
  293 |   expect(body).not.toContain('Whoops');
  294 |   console.log('✅ Stage 4 — Intake complete');
  295 | });
  296 | 
  297 | // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  298 | // STAGE 5 — Billing (Payment Admin Review)
  299 | // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  300 | test('Stage 5 — Billing: Invoice Review', async ({ page }) => {
  301 |   await login(page);
  302 |   await goto(page, `${BASE}/admin/billings`);
  303 |   await lwWait(page, 1000);
  304 |   await snap(page, '05-billing-list');
  305 | 
  306 |   const body = await page.locator('body').textContent();
  307 |   expect(body).not.toContain('403');
  308 |   expect(body).not.toContain('Whoops');
  309 | 
  310 |   const row = page.locator('table tbody tr').first();
  311 |   if (await row.isVisible({ timeout: 4000 }).catch(() => false)) {
  312 |     await row.locator('a').first().click();
  313 |     await lwWait(page, 1000);
  314 |     await snap(page, '05-invoice-detail');
  315 | 
  316 |     // Look for confirm/approve action
  317 |     const actions = ['confirm', 'approve', 'verify'];
  318 |     for (const a of actions) {
  319 |       const btn = page.getByRole('button', { name: new RegExp(a, 'i') }).first();
  320 |       if (await btn.isVisible({ timeout: 1500 }).catch(() => false)) {
  321 |         await btn.click();
  322 |         await lwWait(page, 1500);
  323 |         await snap(page, '05-invoice-confirmed');
  324 |         break;
  325 |       }
  326 |     }
  327 |   } else {
  328 |     console.log('ℹ️  No billing records (expected if no services booked yet)');
  329 |   }
  330 | 
  331 |   console.log('✅ Stage 5 — Billing review complete');
  332 | });
  333 | 
  334 | // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  335 | // STAGE 6 — Cashier: Process Payment
  336 | // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  337 | test('Stage 6 — Cashier: Process Payment', async ({ page }) => {
  338 |   await login(page);
  339 |   await goto(page, `${BASE}/admin/cashier-queues`);
  340 |   await lwWait(page, 1000);
  341 |   await snap(page, '06-cashier-queue');
  342 | 
  343 |   const body = await page.locator('body').textContent();
> 344 |   expect(body).not.toContain('403');
      |                    ^ Error: expect(received).not.toContain(expected) // indexOf
  345 |   expect(body).not.toContain('Whoops');
  346 | 
  347 |   const row = page.locator('table tbody tr').filter({ hasText: new RegExp(LAST, 'i') }).first();
  348 |   if (await row.isVisible({ timeout: 5000 }).catch(() => false)) {
  349 |     await snap(page, '06-client-in-cashier');
  350 | 
  351 |     const payBtn = row.locator('button').filter({ hasText: /pay|collect|process/i }).first();
  352 |     if (await payBtn.isVisible({ timeout: 3000 }).catch(() => false)) {
  353 |       await payBtn.click();
  354 |       await lwWait(page, 1000);
  355 |       await snap(page, '06-payment-modal');
  356 | 
  357 |       // Payment method
  358 |       try {
  359 |         const methodField = page.getByLabel(/Payment Method/i);
  360 |         if (await methodField.isVisible({ timeout: 2000 })) {
  361 |           await filamentSelect(page, 'Payment Method', 'Cash');
  362 |         }
  363 |       } catch { /* optional */ }
  364 | 
  365 |       // Amount
  366 |       try {
  367 |         const amtField = page.getByLabel(/Amount/i).first();
  368 |         if (await amtField.isVisible({ timeout: 2000 })) await amtField.fill('500');
  369 |       } catch { /* optional */ }
  370 | 
  371 |       const confirmBtn = page.getByRole('button', { name: /confirm|pay|submit/i }).last();
  372 |       if (await confirmBtn.isVisible({ timeout: 3000 }).catch(() => false)) {
  373 |         await confirmBtn.click();
  374 |         await lwWait(page, 2000);
  375 |       }
  376 |       await snap(page, '06-payment-complete');
  377 |     } else {
  378 |       await row.locator('a, button').first().click();
  379 |       await lwWait(page, 1000);
  380 |       await snap(page, '06-cashier-detail');
  381 |     }
  382 |   } else {
  383 |     console.log('ℹ️  Client not in cashier queue (expected if payment not yet due)');
  384 |     await snap(page, '06-cashier-empty');
  385 |   }
  386 | 
  387 |   console.log('✅ Stage 6 — Cashier complete');
  388 | });

  391 | // STAGE 7 — Service Queue & Specialist Hub
  392 | // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  393 | test('Stage 7 — Service Queue: Open Specialist Hub', async ({ page }) => {
  394 |   await login(page);
  395 |   await goto(page, `${BASE}/admin/service-queues`);
  396 |   await lwWait(page, 1000);
  397 |   await snap(page, '07-service-queue');
  398 | 
  399 |   const body = await page.locator('body').textContent();
  400 |   expect(body).not.toContain('403');
  401 |   expect(body).not.toContain('Whoops');
  402 | 
  403 |   const row = page.locator('table tbody tr').filter({ hasText: new RegExp(LAST, 'i') }).first();
  404 |   if (await row.isVisible({ timeout: 5000 }).catch(() => false)) {
  405 |     const hubBtn = row.locator('button, a').filter({ hasText: /hub|open/i }).first();
  406 |     if (await hubBtn.isVisible({ timeout: 3000 }).catch(() => false)) {
  407 |       await hubBtn.click();
  408 |       await lwWait(page, 2000);
  409 |       await snap(page, '07-specialist-hub');
  410 |       const hubBody = await page.locator('body').textContent();
  411 |       expect(hubBody).not.toContain('Whoops');
  412 |       console.log('✅ Specialist Hub opened');
  413 |     } else {
  414 |       await row.locator('a, button').first().click();
  415 |       await lwWait(page, 1000);
  416 |       await snap(page, '07-service-row-opened');
  417 |     }
  418 |   } else {
  419 |     console.log('ℹ️  Client not in service queue yet');
  420 |     await goto(page, `${BASE}/admin/service-point-dashboards`);
  421 |     await lwWait(page, 800);
  422 |     await snap(page, '07-service-dashboard');
  423 |   }
  424 | 
  425 |   console.log('✅ Stage 7 — Service queue step complete');
  426 | });
```
